###########################
# South-African TFV events Events
###########################

add_namespace = release_nation_events
country_event = {
	id = release_nation_events.60
	title = release_nation_events.60.t	# Freedom for ANG
	desc = release_nation_events.60.d	#
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.60.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				controls_state = 540 
			}
			AN0 = { transfer_state = 540 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = release_not_local_rulers
			}
			AN0 = { set_government_to_root = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_puppet
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_reichsprotectorate
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_dominion
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion } }
			AN0 = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = ROOT_released_us } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_imperial_protectorate
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_protectorate } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_imperial_associate
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_associate } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_supervised_state
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_supervised_state } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_satellite
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_satellite } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_reichskommissariat
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_colony
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_colony } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_integrated_puppet
			}
			ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = AN0 autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_faction_member
			}
			AN0 = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = ROOT_released_us } }
			ROOT = { add_to_faction = AN0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = release_as_free
			}
			AN0 = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = ROOT_released_us } }
		}
		ROOT = {
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = am.news.6 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.nevermind
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = release_nation_events.110
	title = release_nation_events.110.t	# Hamilton
	desc = release_nation_events.110.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		332 = {
			OWNER = {
				save_event_target_as = owner_of_labrador
			}
		}
		466 = {
			OWNER = {
				save_event_target_as = owner_of_new_quebec
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.110.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = event_target:owner_of_labrador }
			event_target:owner_of_labrador = {
				controls_state = 332
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				controls_state = 855
				NOT = { original_tag = QUE }
			}
			event_target:owner_of_labrador = {
				transfer_state = 855
			}
		}
		if = {	
			limit = {
				event_target:owner_of_labrador = {
					NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = gave_labrador }
					NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = gave_newfoundland_and_labrador }
				}
			}
			event_target:owner_of_labrador = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = gave_hamilton }
			}
		}
		event_target:owner_of_labrador = {
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = am.news.66 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.110.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					NOT = { tag = event_target:owner_of_labrador }
					event_target:owner_of_labrador = {
						controls_state = 332
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = event_target:owner_of_new_quebec }
			event_target:owner_of_new_quebec = {
				controls_state = 466
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				controls_state = 855
				NOT = { original_tag = QUE }
			}
			event_target:owner_of_new_quebec = {
				transfer_state = 855
			}
		}
		if = {	
			limit = {
				event_target:owner_of_new_quebec = {
					NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = gave_labrador }
					NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = gave_newfoundland_and_labrador }
				}
			}
			event_target:owner_of_new_quebec = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = gave_hamilton }
			}
		}
		event_target:owner_of_new_quebec = {
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = am.news.67 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.nevermind
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

					}

							has_country_flag = release_as_reichskommissariat
						}

					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_colony
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = PL5 autonomy_state = autonomy_colony } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_integrated_puppet
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = PL5 autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet } }

						}

						}

					}
					ROOT = {

						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

			factor = 0
		}

					exists = yes
					has_cosmetic_tag = PLU_south_pacific_mandate
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = hold_referendum_plu_and_mcr_tooltip
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { original_tag = MCR }
				MC5 = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = hold_referendum_only_mcr_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = hold_referendum_only_plu_tooltip
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							controls_state = 882
						}
						CK5 = {
							transfer_state = 882
							if = {
								limit = {
									ROOT = {
										original_tag = JAP
									}
								}
								set_country_flag = released_by_japan_flag
								hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_CHU_JAP" }
							}
							else = {
								hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_CHU" }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							882 = {
								is_core_of = PL5
							}
						}
						PL5 = {
							remove_state_core = 882
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							has_country_flag = release_not_local_rulers
						}
						CK5 = { set_government_to_root = yes }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_puppet
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_reichsprotectorate
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_dominion
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion } }
						CK5 = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = ROOT_released_us } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_imperial_protectorate
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_protectorate } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_imperial_associate
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_associate } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_supervised_state
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_supervised_state } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_satellite
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_satellite } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_reichskommissariat
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_colony
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_colony } }
					}

							has_country_flag = release_as_integrated_puppet
						}
						ROOT = { set_autonomy = { target = CK5 autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet } }
					}
					else_if = {

							has_country_flag = release_as_faction_member
						}
						CK5 = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = ROOT_released_us } }
						ROOT = { add_to_faction = CK5 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = release_as_free
						}
						CK5 = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = ROOT_released_us } }
					}
					ROOT = {
						hidden_effect = {
							news_event = { id = am.news.94 days = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							original_tag = PLU
							PL5 = { exists = no }
							PL5 = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = PLU_south_pacific_mandate } }
							PL5 = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							controls_state = 882
						}
						PL5 = {
							transfer_state = 882
							hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_CHU_PLU" }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							882 = {
								NOT = { is_core_of = PL5 }
							}
						}
						PL5 = {
							add_state_core = 882
						}
					}
					PL5 = {
						add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = gave_truk }
					}
					ROOT = {
						hidden_effect = {
							news_event = { id = am.news.96 days = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				70 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							original_tag = MCR
							MC5 = { exists = no }
							MC5 = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							controls_state = 882
						}
						MC5 = {
							transfer_state = 882
							hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_CHU_PLU" }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							882 = {
								is_core_of = PL5
							}
						}
						PL5 = {
							remove_state_core = 882
						}
					}
					MC5 = {
						MCR_add_stars = yes
						add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = gave_truk }
					}
					ROOT = {
						hidden_effect = {
							news_event = { id = am.news.95 days = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.nevermind
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
